DSSSB Admit Card 2025 Released for Various Post Codes
ЁЯФЧ тАв DSSSB has released the admit cards for various post code examinations scheduled between June 23 to July 9, 2025. Candidates can download their hall tickets from the official website dsssb.delhi.gov.in by entering their application number and date of birth. CG Vyapam Peon Bharti 2025 Online Form
ЁЯФЧ тАв Chhattisgarh Professional Examination Board (CG Vyapam) has released the MLV125 Recruitment 2025 notification for various Group D posts under the Department of Printing and Stationery, Raipur. A total of 19 vacancies are available for positions such as Darkroom Assistant, Pasting Boy, Auxiliary, Inkman/Inker, Junior Binder, Hamal, Sweeper, Watchman, Mortuary Attendant, and Helper. Candidates who have passed 5th or 8th class and possess relevant experience (as per the post) are eligible to apply. Both male and female candidates can submit their applications online through the official website of CG Vyapam. The online application process is open from 27 June 2025 to 25 July 2025. Applicants must ensure to review the official notification carefully and complete the form, including uploading documents and paying the fee online. The written exam is tentatively scheduled for 31 August 2025 at district centers like Raipur, Durg, and Bilaspur.

ЁЯФЧ тАв The Railway Recruitment Board (RRB) has released the RRB Technician Recruitment 2025 notification for Technician Grade-1 (Signal) and Technician Grade-3 (Open Line) posts. RRB ALP CBAT Exam Admit Card 2025
ЁЯФЧ тАв The Railway Recruitment Board (RRB) has officially announced the exam date for the Computer-Based Aptitude Test (CBAT) under the Assistant Loco Pilot (ALP) recruitment, CEN 01/2024. The CBAT exam is scheduled to be held on 15th July 2025. Candidates who qualified in CBT-2 are eligible to appear for this final stage. The City Intimation Slip is expected to be released from 5th July 2025, and the admit cards will likely be available from 11th July 2025. Aadhaar-based biometric verification will be mandatory on the exam day. For more details, candidates are advised to visit the official RRB website at rrbcdg.gov.in.

CG Abkari Aarakshak Bharti 2025 Online Form
ЁЯФЧ тАв CG Abkari Aarakshak Bharti 2025 invites applications for 200 Excise Constable posts. Eligible candidates who have passed 12th can apply online from June 4 to June 27, 2025. The written exam will be held on July 27, 2025. Applicants from all Indian states can apply, but only Chhattisgarh residents will receive reservation and age relaxation benefits. The recruitment will be conducted by CG Vyapam, and the selection process includes a written test and physical eligibility test.
